msg:Stayed at this hotel last minute due to a canceled train. Arrived after 8pm. The location is really convenient. It's walking distance from Xuzhou East Station. The staff was really friendly though not much was available around the hotel. The bar and both restaurants were not able to provide drinks. Fortunately there are many shops and restaurants around the hotel so if you are in need you can make do. They are willing to provide assistance ordering anything you may need through delivery services 24 hours a day so that too is an option. Lastly, the gym is really great and very clean however when I went to go look for for Sauna the men's locker room was locked and the women's locker room had a staff member sleeping in it so we weren't sure what that area of the hotel was like. 

Obviously this was around 9 o'clock at night so it's hard to know what it's like during the day.
